47:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["Stateful property testing — generates random sequences of commands, with automatic shrinking on failure. Uses ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"step.allActions"}]," to generate both transaction submissions (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"SubmitTxCommand"}],") and slot advancements (",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AdvanceSlotCommand"}],")."]}]
48:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["This is the right choice when the exploration space is too large for exhaustive Scenario exploration. Instead of checking every combination, ScalaCheck randomly samples N command sequences (controlled by ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"withMinSuccessfulTests"}],"), each time picking a random action from ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"allActions"}],". If a violation is found, ScalaCheck automatically shrinks the sequence to the minimal failing case. This trades completeness for scalability — you can test contracts with hundreds of participants, dozens of actions, and complex time-dependent logic where exhaustive exploration would be infeasible."]}]
